window.__googleInit = function() {

    if (window.mapInstance != null) {
        return;
    }

    window.mapContainer = document.createElement('div');
    window.mapContainer.style.height = '100%';
    window.mapContainer.style.width = '100%';
    window.mapContainer.style.visibility = 'hidden';

    document.body.appendChild(window.mapContainer);

    
    window.mapInstance = new google.maps.Map(
        window.mapContainer,
        {
            gestureHandling: 'cooperative',
            backgroundColor: 'rgba(229, 227, 223, 1)',
            mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP,
            controlSize: 28,
            disableDefaultUI: true,
            zoomControl: false,
            zoomControlOptions: {
                position: google.maps.ControlPosition.TOP_LEFT,
            },
            styles: [
                {
                    featureType: 'poi',
                    elementType: 'labels',
                    stylers: [{ visibility: 'off' }],
                },
                {
                    featureType: 'administrative.neighborhood',
                    elementType: 'all',
                    stylers: [{ visibility: 'off' }],
                },
            ],
        }
    );

    var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
        position: {lat: 0, lng: 0},
        map: window.mapInstance,
    });
    marker.setMap(null);
    window.mapInstance.setCenter({lat: 0, lng: 0});


    if(window.__mapReady) {
        window.__mapReady();
    }
}

                requestIdleCallback(addCookieManagementScript, { timeout: 4000 });
            } else {
                setTimeout(addCookieManagementScript, 2000);
            }
        </script><script type="text/javascript">window.yelp.initReactComponents();</script></body></html>
